 1

 3
 To remove hairiness, massage oil in hair once a week
 4

 5

 ) If you are fond of food and onion is an important part of your taste, then you must have shed tears many times while cutting onion
 pyaaj khaane main jitna swaadisht lagata he, katate samay utana hi rulaata he
 But if you want, you can cut onions without crying by adopting some easy remedies
 kyon aate hai aansu?pyaaj kaatane ke dauraan ek chemical ri-ection hota he or gas nikalati he
 When this gas comes in contact with water, acid is formed
 isi vajah se hamaari ankhon main jalan hone lagati he
 But if you want, you can avoid this problem by taking some small measures before cutting onions
 1
 Chill the onion and cut, peel off the onion
 iske baad use kuch der ke liye pani main dubokar chhod den
 Cut the onion after half an hour
 aisa karne se ankhon main jalan nahin hogi
 But because of keeping it in water, onion will become sticky
 aise main puri saavdhaanee se pyaaj kaaten
 2
 vinegar kaa bhi istemaal kar sakate hanaap chahen to pyaaj ko chhilakar kuch der ke liye vinegar or pani ke ghol main bhi dubokar rakh sakate hai
 Doing this will not cause tears in eyes
 3
 After keeping it in the fridge, remove the peel of the interest and keep it in the fridge for some time
 iske baad pyaaj kaaten
 However, this method is not very popular because doing so smells in the fridge
 4
 Cut the top of the onion, everyone has their own way of cutting the onion
 lekin pyaaj kaatane kaa sabase sahi tarika ye he ki ham pyaaj ke sabase upree hisse ko pehle katkar nikaal den
 Cutting the onion will be much easier after cutting off the top
